prompt Creating DDC_APPROVE_USER...
create table DDC_APPROVE_USER
(
  id              NUMBER not null,
  user_name       VARCHAR2(50),
  user_orgname    VARCHAR2(50),
  user_role_name  VARCHAR2(200),
  approve_index   NUMBER,
  approve_note    VARCHAR2(500),
  approve_table   VARCHAR2(100),
  approve_tableid NUMBER,
  approve_time    DATE,
  approve_state   NUMBER,
  lsh             VARCHAR2(100),
  syn_flag        VARCHAR2(10),
  tran_date       DATE,
  approve_no      VARCHAR2(100)
)
;
comment on table DDC_APPROVE_USER
  is '审批人意见表';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.id
  is '主键';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.user_name
  is '用户姓名';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.user_orgname
  is '用户部门';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.user_role_name
  is '用户角色';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.approve_index
  is '用户审批顺序';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.approve_note
  is '用户审批备注';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.approve_table
  is '审批表名';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.approve_tableid
  is '审批表名ID';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.approve_time
  is '审批时间';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.approve_state
  is '审批意见 0-同意 1-拒绝';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.lsh
  is '流水号';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.syn_flag
  is '同步标志';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.tran_date
  is '传送时间';
comment on column DDC_APPROVE_USER.approve_no
  is '审批编号(唯一)';
alter table DDC_APPROVE_USER
  add constraint PK_DDC_APPROVE_USER primary key (ID);
alter table DDC_APPROVE_USER
  add constraint UN_APPROVE_NO unique (APPROVE_NO);

create table DDC_DAXXB
(
  id                NUMBER not null,
  dabh              VARCHAR2(50) not null,
  ywlx              VARCHAR2(20),
  ywyy              VARCHAR2(20),
  hyxhzh            VARCHAR2(20),
  ssdwid            VARCHAR2(500),
  cphm              VARCHAR2(50),
  ppxh              VARCHAR2(50),
  cysy              VARCHAR2(20),
  djh               VARCHAR2(50),
  jtzz              VARCHAR2(20),
  jsrxm1            VARCHAR2(20),
  xb1               VARCHAR2(20),
  sfzmhm1           VARCHAR2(20),
  lxdh1             VARCHAR2(20),
  jsrxm2            VARCHAR2(20),
  xb2               VARCHAR2(20),
  sfzmhm2           VARCHAR2(20),
  lxdh2             VARCHAR2(20),
  jsrxm3            VARCHAR2(20),
  xb3               VARCHAR2(20),
  sfzmhm3           VARCHAR2(20),
  lxdh3             VARCHAR2(20),
  xsqy              VARCHAR2(20),
  bz                VARCHAR2(200),
  zt                VARCHAR2(10),
  syrq              DATE,
  slzl              VARCHAR2(100),
  slyj              VARCHAR2(20),
  slbz              VARCHAR2(100),
  slr               VARCHAR2(20),
  slrq              DATE,
  slbm              VARCHAR2(20),
  gdyj              VARCHAR2(20),
  tbyy              CHAR(10),
  gdbz              VARCHAR2(100),
  gdr               VARCHAR2(20),
  gdrq              DATE,
  gdbm              VARCHAR2(20),
  syn_flag          VARCHAR2(10),
  tran_flag         VARCHAR2(10),
  tran_date         DATE,
  vc_user1img       VARCHAR2(100),
  vc_user2img       VARCHAR2(100),
  vc_ebike_img      VARCHAR2(100),
  vc_user1_cardimg1 VARCHAR2(100),
  vc_user1_cardimg2 VARCHAR2(100),
  vc_user2_cardimg1 VARCHAR2(100),
  vc_user2_cardimg2 VARCHAR2(100),
  vc_ebike_invoice  VARCHAR2(100)
)
;
comment on table DDC_DAXXB
  is '电动车档案信息表';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.dabh
  is '新进入的数据，自动生成档案编号4403 00000001；老数据去更新';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.ywlx
  is '业务类型';

  is '车牌号码，办结后，以流水转入本表的车牌号码数据填充本表';

  is '驾驶人姓名3';

  is '性别3';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.sfzmhm3
  is '身份证号码3';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.lxdh3
  is '联系电话3';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.xsqy
  is '行驶区域(福田区、罗湖区.....)';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.bz
  is '备注';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.zt
  is '车辆状态 填字典';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.syrq
  is '审验日期：新车归档日期+2年或年审验车合格后的归档日期+2年';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.slzl
  is '受理资料，分割 字典表';

  is '受理意见 0 同意 1 不同意 特别注意 档案更正是要填写本表记录';

  is '受理备注';

  is '受理人';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.slrq
  is '受理日期';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.slbm
  is '受理部门';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.gdyj
  is '归档意见 0 办结 1 退办 成功办结的信息才会进入本表';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.tbyy
  is '退办原因';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.gdbz
  is '归档备注';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.gdr
  is '归档人';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.gdrq
  is '归档日期';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.gdbm
  is '归档部门';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.syn_flag
  is '同步标志,填写规则详看其他文档';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.tran_flag
  is '传送标志(该字段必须有索引)';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.tran_date
  is '传送时间';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.vc_user1img
  is '驾驶人照片1';
comment on column DDC_DAXXB.vc_user2img
  is '驾驶人照片2';

  is '车辆照片';

prompt Creating DDC_DRIVER...
create table DDC_DRIVER
(
  id            NUMBER not null,
  dabh          VARCHAR2(50),
  daid          NUMBER,
  jsrxm         VARCHAR2(50),
  xb            VARCHAR2(50),
  lxdh          VARCHAR2(50),
  syn_flag      VARCHAR2(50),
  tran_date     DATE default sysdate,
  user_code     VARCHAR2(50),
  user_password VARCHAR2(50),
  sfzhm         VARCHAR2(50),
  vcuser_img    VARCHAR2(100)
)
;
comment on table DDC_DRIVER
  is '司机表';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.id
  is '主键';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.dabh
  is '档案编号';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.daid
  is '档案表ID';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.jsrxm
  is '姓名';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.xb
  is '性别';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.lxdh
  is '联系电话';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.syn_flag
  is '传送标志';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.tran_date
  is '传送时间';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.user_code
  is '用户名';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.user_password
  is '用户密码';
comment on column DDC_DRIVER.sfzhm
  is '身份证号码';
alter table DDC_DRIVER
  add constraint PK_DDC_DRIVER primary key (ID);

(
  id            NUMBER not null,
  user_code     VARCHAR2(20),
  user_password VARCHAR2(20),
  user_name     VARCHAR2(20),
  user_org      VARCHAR2(150),
  user_state    VARCHAR2(2),
  user_role     VARCHAR2(100),
  op_ip         VARCHAR2(20),
  op_date       VARCHAR2(50),
